public class Estudiante {
    private String codigo;
    private String nombre;
    private String carreraCodigo;
    private int creditosAprobados;
    private String planEstudioCodigo;

    public Estudiante(String codigo, String nombre, String carreraCodigo, int creditosAprobados, String planEstudioCodigo) {
        this.codigo = codigo;
        this.nombre = nombre;
        this.carreraCodigo = carreraCodigo;
        this.creditosAprobados = creditosAprobados;
        this.planEstudioCodigo = planEstudioCodigo;
    }

    // Getters y Setters
    public String getCodigo() {
        return codigo;
    }

    public String getNombre() {
        return nombre;
    }

    public String getCarreraCodigo() {
        return carreraCodigo;
    }

    public int getCreditosAprobados() {
        return creditosAprobados;
    }

    public String getPlanEstudioCodigo() {
        return planEstudioCodigo;
    }
}

8/5/2025, 5:43â€¯p.â€¯m. - Fer: package demomq10java21;

import org.apache.activemq.artemis.api.jms.ActiveMQJMSClient;
import com.google.gson.Gson;
import javax.jms.*;

public class JmsEmisorGenericoTopic {

    public static void enviarMensaje(String topicName, Object obj) throws Exception {
        Gson gson = new Gson();
        String json = gson.toJson(obj);

        String url = "tcp://localhost:61616";
        ConnectionFactory cf = ActiveMQJMSClient.createConnectionFactory(url, null);
        Connection connection = cf.createConnection("admin", "admin");
        connection.start();

        Session session = connection.createSession(false, Session.AUTO_ACKNOWLEDGE);
        Topic topic = session.createTopic(topicName);
        MessageProducer producer = session.createProducer(topic);

        TextMessage msg = session.createTextMessage(json);
        msg.setJMSDeliveryMode(DeliveryMode.PERSISTENT);

        System.out.println("ðŸ“¤ Enviando mensaje al topic: " + topicName);
        producer.send(msg);

        session.close();
        connection.close();
    }
}
 este es el emisor genÃ©rico topic

import java.util.List;

public class MainEnvioTopic {
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        try {
            String topicName = "mqluis_estudiantes";

            // Crear estudiantes de ejemplo
            List<EstudianteEgresado> estudiantes = List.of(
                    new EstudianteEgresado("20210001", "Luis Perez", "CS", 180, "2018"),
                    new EstudianteEgresado("20210002", "Ana Lopez", "IT", 190, "2019"),
                    new EstudianteEgresado("20210003", "Carlos Diaz", "CS", 160, "2020"),
                    new EstudianteEgresado("20210004", "Maria PÃ©rez", "IT", 170, "2021")
            );

            // Publicar al topic
            for (EstudianteEgresado estudiante : estudiantes) {
                JmsEmisorGenericoTopic.enviarMensaje(topicName, estudiante);
            }

            System.out.println("âœ… Estudiantes enviados correctamente al topic: " + topicName);

        } catch (Exception e) {
            e.printStackTrace();
        }
    }
}

8/5/2025, 5:44â€¯p.â€¯m. - Fer: y este es un suscrito package demomq10java21;

import javax.jms.*;
import org.apache.activemq.artemis.api.jms.ActiveMQJMSClient;

public class ReceptorCarreraCS {
    public static void main(String[] args) throws Exception {
        String url = "tcp://localhost:61616";
        ConnectionFactory cf = ActiveMQJMSClient.createConnectionFactory(url, null);
        Connection connection = cf.createConnection("admin", "admin");
        connection.start();

        Session session = connection.createSession(false, Session.AUTO_ACKNOWLEDGE);
        Topic topic = session.createTopic("mqluis_estudiantes");
        MessageConsumer consumer = session.createConsumer(topic, "carreraCodigo = 'CS'");

        System.out.println("â³ Esperando estudiantes de CS...");
        consumer.setMessageListener(message -> {
            if (message instanceof TextMessage) {
                try {
                    String json = ((TextMessage) message).getText();
                    System.out.println("ðŸ“¥ Estudiante recibido en CS: " + json);
                } catch (Exception e) {
                    e.printStackTrace();
                }
            }
        });
    }
